Song Ziwen Eloquently Discusses Northwest Development in Lanzhou; Hu Junzhuang Injured in Horseback Fall 22

(Lanzhou) All sectors of Lanzhou held a grand welcome meeting for Song Ziwen on the morning of the 5th. Song's speech was as follows: "Chairman, fellow brothers, it is a great pleasure to meet with the compatriots of Gansu in Lanzhou today. I just heard the chairman's welcoming remarks, which were overly complimentary to me. While I am very grateful, I also feel very ashamed. Two weeks ago, I entered Tongguan from the capital and was very satisfied with what I saw and heard in various aspects of Shaanxi because, although materially poor, the people's spirits are extremely high and very different from a few years ago. Everyone is full of vigor and hope for recovery, not the kind of sitting around waiting for death that I saw in the 18th and 19th years of the Republic. Now that I have arrived in Gansu, everything I have seen gives me the same impression of the entire Northwest. I believe that the future of the Northwest is very bright. People from other provinces who come to the Northwest for inspection generally have two kinds of impressions. One is to vigorously praise the profound culture of the Northwest and to view the Northwest with the eyes of a writer or poet. The other is to criticize the backwardness of production, the lack of education, and the poverty of the people, viewing the Northwest with the eyes of a foreigner. I believe that both attitudes are biased and inappropriate. The prosperous and glorious history of the Northwest in the past was the result of the efforts of our ancestors. We cannot only remember the achievements of our ancestors; we must be ashamed of the uselessness of our descendants. Thinking about the past and forgetting the present means forgetting to continue the efforts of our ancestors in the future. At the same time, we must know that our entire China is a backward country. Although the southeastern provinces are more advanced than the northwestern provinces, they are still unable to advance like the great powers every day. Moreover, the current material progress in the southeastern provinces is not because the people of the southeast are more intelligent or hardworking than the people of the northwest. It is entirely due to the geographical advantages of the southeast, because the coastal provinces have convenient transportation and can absorb the economic and scientific forces of Europe and the West. If the northwestern provinces can also use the economic and scientific forces of Europe and the West, they will certainly be able to restore local prosperity and consolidate the foundation of the country in a short period of time. The construction of the Northwest is not a local problem; it is a problem for the entire country. Now that the provinces along the Yangtze River and the coast are already under the fire of invaders, we

should quickly pay attention to construction in the Northwest hinterland, the birthplace of the Chinese nation. After the European War, Turkey, in a very dangerous situation, moved its capital from the prosperous Constantinople to Ankara, the birthplace of the Turkish nation. Our country, in a time of extreme crisis, should also pay attention to construction in the Northwest hinterland, the birthplace of our nation. The Central Government attaches great importance to the construction of the Northwest. Chairman Chiang and President Wang are unable to attend to military and political affairs, so I have been commissioned by the Economic Commission to represent all the standing committee members and come to

the Northwest for inspection. The construction of the Northwest is a huge topic, and there are many things that should be done. The Economic Commission is suffering from limited resources and can only select urgent and basic tasks and do them step by step. What we have planned is, first, the roads for transportation with the Southeast. Before the Longhai Railway is completed, we will first build the highways, plan the transportation methods perfectly, and bring in the economic power of the Southeast and the science of Europe and the West. Second, there is water conservancy work that will benefit farmers and reduce disasters. We have already discussed the canal opening plan with Director Xu of the Construction Department. The third is the improvement of agricultural products. The fourth is the implementation of sanitation and the organization of veterinary medicine. The Economic Commission has roughly drafted plans for these four undertakings, and the Provincial Government has allocated Xiaoxihu as the general office for Gansu Province. Construction undertakings certainly require planning and considerable financial resources, but at the same time, it also requires the cooperation of the entire country to achieve a bright path. Chairman Zhu has a very long history with the Party and the country and has deep experience in military and political affairs. In less than a year of governing Gansu, the politics and security of Gansu Province have made good progress. The people of Gansu are already in the process of recovery. This is a foundation for successful construction. Yesterday, I also had talks with leaders from all walks of life and gained many benefits. However, I am still not very familiar with the local situation. Before I leave Gansu Province, I hope that comrades from all walks of life can provide guidance and assistance at any time. After I leave Gansu Province, I also ask that you provide the same guidance and assistance to Director Liu Jingshan of the Northwest

Office of the Economic Commission. I dare to make a judgment that with such an enlightened leader as Chairman Zhu and the assistance of comrades from all walks of life, construction will certainly proceed smoothly and quickly yield results. The construction of the Northwest is the lifeline of the Republic of China. The responsibility borne by the people of the Northwest is not only to enrich their own interests. I hope that my compatriots from all walks of life, under the leadership of the government and the Party, will unite as one and devote all their efforts to the Northwest construction that will save the country and the people." (Seventh dispatch from the Central News Agency)

(Lanzhou) For Song Ziwen's inspection of the Northwest, Hu Junzhuang of the Shanghai banking community was invited by Song to come and inspect the commerce of the Northwest. Song went deep into the interior of Shaanxi and Gansu. He personally investigated and studied Xianyang, Jingyang, Wugong, Qishan, Fufeng, Xingping, Baoji, Fengxiang, and other counties in central Shaanxi Province. After arriving in Lanzhou, he went to the countryside every day for on-site inspections. On the morning of the 6th, he flew to Xining, but the plane could not take off due to rain and damage. He then rode horses with Zhu Shaoliang, Deng Baoshan, Zhu Duomin, Hu Junzhuang, Liu Jingshan, and others to inspect the area dozens of miles outside the city. When passing through a mountain road in Gucheng, the packhorse lost its footing and fell. Hu was crushed, fracturing his right leg, and immediately fainted and lost consciousness. His companions carried Hu back to the provincial government. Wang, the director of Zhongshan Hospital, and Dr. Siba, a League of Nations health expert who came with him, examined him and found that his right leg was broken. Surgery was performed immediately to set the bone, and his condition was good. He was also conscious. According to the two doctors, Hu's horsemanship was fortunately good, and only his leg was injured. According to the injury, there is no danger to his life, but there is no orthopedic equipment for treatment in Lanzhou, so he must return to Shanghai. After five or six weeks, the leg bone can be completely restored. He is scheduled to return to Shanghai by plane this Thursday. At that time, rumors spread in Lanzhou that Song himself was injured, and all parties were shocked. Many people went to the provincial government to inquire. The rumors were dispelled after the news was disclosed in the newspaper. (Eighth dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Internal Disputes in the British Cabinet Over Disarmament; Henderson Goes to Geneva to Prepare for the Meeting 30

(London) After the Cabinet Disarmament Committee met this morning, Prime Minister MacDonald summoned other cabinet members to hold an emergency cabinet meeting. The convening of this emergency meeting is said to be due to a conflict between two factions in the cabinet. The Prime Minister MacDonald and Lord Privy Seal Baldwin faction advocate that the disarmament treaty must be linked to a wide range of safeguards, but several other cabinet members, such as the ministers in charge of national defense, oppose proceeding with disarmament talks. Since the recent debate on the disarmament issue in the House of Commons, the dispute between the two factions in the cabinet has intensified. The convening of this emergency cabinet meeting may be because the Cabinet Disarmament Committee has already reached a consensus and submitted a disarmament policy to all cabinet members for a vote. Whether they can agree to this approach must be expressed immediately by all cabinet members. Although details are still difficult to ascertain, one thing is clear: that the British cabinet is concerned with, nominally, the disarmament issue, but will henceforth focus on planning for the security of Great Britain. (Eighth dispatch from Havas)

(Geneva) Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson is scheduled to depart from London for Paris tomorrow and then from Paris to Geneva to prepare for the General Committee meeting of the Disarmament Conference on May 29. (Eighth dispatch from Havas)

Aircraft Parts Sold to Germany, France Asks England for Explanation, Wu Fang Claims Commercial Nature Cannot be Prohibited 31

(London) The "Daily Mail" reported on the 23rd of last month that some British manufacturers were preparing to sell aircraft engines to Germany. According to sources in the British aviation industry, the French government, based on the above news, has requested an explanation from the British government. Relevant French parties believe that if this matter proves to be true, then this behavior is completely contrary to the exchange of views between the British and French governments on the issue of disarmament and the speeches repeatedly made by British politicians. British officials said that civil aviation parts are entirely within the scope of commerce and the government cannot prohibit their sale, and there is no charter that can distinguish between military and civil aircraft parts. British people are now advocating the establishment of a disarmament convention to determine the nature of various aviation equipment and their manufacturing parts. (7th Havas dispatch)

He advocated that the citizens' election should be postponed immediately until the protection is sufficiently increased, but Bo did not mention how the protection can be considered sufficient. England's Position in the Far East, the Focus of Parliamentary Debate, the Government's Deference to Japan, Labor Party Members' Severe Criticism, Simon Distorts the Meaning of Japan's Special Rights 33

(London) Lord Pengsonby submitted a motion in the Upper House today, strongly advocating a more resolute Far East policy, especially regarding armaments. Pengsonby declared that newspapers are rumored that the Japanese Imperial Family should ask England, with the intention of examining England's guns and cannons. The Japanese Imperial Family has ordered guns and cannons from armories, which is undoubtedly true. These guns and cannons will obviously be used to deal with the British army. Pengsonby continued that Japan's recent warning to other countries not to interfere in Chinese affairs is tantamount to announcing the Monroe Doctrine of East Asia. England's every submission to Japan's demands is also unfavorable to the whole world. However, after Foreign Affairs Second Secretary Stenhope explained England's position, Pengsonby withdrew his proposal. Stenhope stated that the British government is satisfied with Japan's declaration to abide by the Nine-Power Treaty and the Open Door Policy in China. Regarding the active action taken by Britain in the Far East, Lord Stenhope said that without the cooperation of the United States, any restrictive action is impossible, and the United States has no indication of considering this action. Since Japan's recent declaration and the failure of the Anglo-Japanese Trade Conference, England's position in the Far East has been the focus of parliamentary debate. (7th National News Agency dispatch)

(London) The House of Lords held a meeting today and had a lengthy and broad debate on the Far East issue and the disarmament issue. This debate was caused by the resolution of Lord Pengsonby, a member of the Labor Party. Pengsonby's resolution was based on the fact that the current Far East and disarmament issues are quite worrying, so he asked the government to adopt a more active policy on these two issues. When Pengsonby explained the case, he questioned the government, saying that Japan's actions clearly violated various international treaties. Japan's occupation of several provinces of China by force and its separation from the rest of China are undoubtedly in conflict with the Nine-Power Treaty, but the British government is surprised that it seems to be satisfied with this situation and the Japanese government's recent response to British negotiations. Then Lord Cecil, the former representative to the League of Nations, spoke, saying that currently, except for Japan, all countries do not want to destroy peace, so the danger of an immediate outbreak of war does not seem to exist, but the concerns mentioned by Pengsonby earlier are indeed justified. The government's remarks are sometimes quite strong and active, but its actions have always been very weak. At this point, Foreign Affairs Second Secretary Stenhope stood up to defend the government, saying that the accusations of the members are not appropriate. England cannot independently make any initiatives on the Manchuria Incident. Although the United States took action alone in January 1932, (referring to the fact that when the Japanese army attacked Jinzhou, the United States sent the same type of note to China and Japan, requesting respect for the Nine-Power Treaty,) but it must be known that the United States does not join the League of Nations, while England is a member of the League of Nations. Since China has appealed to Geneva, England cannot act alone, and the Lytton Investigation Team and the Advisory Committee on Sino-Japanese Affairs of the League of Nations have not advocated sanctions against Japan, and England is not in a position to disagree. Finally, Stenhope said that the government's recent reply from Japan is considered satisfactory, which is completely correct. The Japanese reply expresses respect for the Nine-Power Treaty and the principle of the Open Door, and England should naturally consider it satisfactory. (7th Havas dispatch)

(Nanjing) A London dispatch stated that Foreign Minister Simon, in response to a question in the House of Commons, stated that "Japan's special rights and interests in China that are recognized by other countries but not shared by other countries" means that if the Japanese oppose any special policies of the British government towards China, or oppose any special activities of the British in China, it must be pointed out that this policy or activity infringes on some special rights and interests of Japan, and that these rights and interests are recognized by other countries but not shared by other countries. (General rights and interests do not belong to this category. Japan, like other countries, has obtained special rights and interests in China through the effectiveness of agreements regarding specific operations, which are recognized by other countries but not shared by other countries, such as the Japanese Concession in Hankou. These agreements cannot be listed one by one now, and there is no need to list them one by one, because the responsibility for distinguishing what is a special right and interest and what is not lies not with the British government.) Simon continued in response to another question that if Japan's desire is only to express opposition to hindering the peace and order of East Asia, then he hopes that all signatories to the Nine-Power Treaty will have the same purpose. (8th Central News Agency dispatch)

US Requests to Establish Naval Coal Station, Rejected by Mexico 36

Establish Air Police to Crack Down on Private Smuggling of Drugs by Aircraft, US Representative Proposes to the League of Nations 37

(Geneva) The League of Nations is currently investigating whether to establish an international air police force to crack down on the illegal transportation of narcotic drugs by aircraft. This case was proposed to the League of Nations by Fuller, the US State Department's opium director and US representative to the League of Nations opium conference. After being approved by the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations, Exeterland, the director of the League of Nations opium department, immediately sought opinions from various governments. Fuller declared to the League of Nations Advisory Committee on Opium that the United States attaches great importance to the use of aircraft to smuggle drugs. The committee also expressed concern as a result. In a letter to various governments, Exeterland asked governments to report to the League of Nations the entire situation of illegal air transportation of drugs in their countries, as well as measures to crack down on it. Based on the reports received, the League of Nations will recommend the establishment of air police to prevent this type of air smuggling. The US representative said that the United States has discovered that a considerable number of drugs are transported by air from Canada. These aircraft are purely privately owned and fly out of Canadian airfields. When taking off, the cargo loaded in the aircraft is legal goods, but in the middle of the journey, they land somewhere, drop illegal goods in, and then fly to a designated location in the United States to unload the goods. The empty aircraft then flies back to Canada along the original route. Therefore, the only way to crack down on it is to use aircraft to patrol. The United States has now established this type of air police in many places. In the first year of its establishment (1932), 35 smuggling aircraft were captured. Most of the smuggled goods were alcohol. In the following year, 30 smuggling aircraft were captured in six months. However, it is extremely difficult to investigate drugs, because smugglers can drop or destroy drugs in the air in advance. However, the amount of drugs seized by the government is still very considerable. Opium experts believe that although a large number of drugs in Europe are smuggled by air, several cases have been seized on commercial aircraft, but so far there is no air police force equipment. (8th National News Agency dispatch)

France Emulates Roosevelt's Five-Year Revival Plan, Manages Production and Distribution, Funding Requires 100 Million Francs, Will be Submitted to Congress for Discussion 38

(Paris) Representative and Mayor Haver presented to the House of Representatives a five-year plan for the development of French agriculture, industry and commerce. An Associated Press reporter learned that some major French industries are now considering implementing a plan to manage production and distribution. This type of plan is similar to the National Industrial Recovery Act of the United States and has a validity period of three years or more. Meyer's plan stipulates that the minimum amount of funding within five years is 10,000,000,000 francs. Part of the funding comes from tax revenue, and the remaining part is borrowed from the National Social Insurance Fund. Its purpose is to subsidize export trade, shipbuilding companies and shipping companies, and the government will also use the fund to support agriculture. The French wine industry has been sluggish in recent years, and the government will pay special attention to it. The plan also stipulates the funding for public works in Algeria, Tunisia, and Morocco to develop railways and new-style commercial ports. The government will also follow the example of the United States and provide low-interest loans to local governments to develop public works in various places. Meyer believes that his plan is also profitable in itself, because most of the expenses can be compensated by reducing unemployment benefits, and the national tax revenue will inevitably be abundant after the revitalization of industry and commerce. After Congress reopens on May 15, it may discuss this five-year plan, and the Du Mayer government may also draft its own plan. If the government decides to draft its own plan, its content will follow the example of President Roosevelt's revival plan. (8th National News Agency dispatch)

England, France, Holland, India, and Siam Sign Rubber Management Agreement, Consumers Will Be Asked to Join in Cooperation, Consult with the International Committee 40

(London) Representatives of England, France, the Netherlands, India, and Siam signed an intergovernmental agreement on the implementation of the Rubber Management Plan at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today. At the same time, the House of Commons also discussed the various points of this agreement. Colonial Secretary Lister said that consumers will be asked to appoint representatives to join a group to advise the International Committee on rubber management matters. The British government had discussed this plan with the US government for a long time before it was announced. He felt that the plan was well-considered and sufficient to obtain a reasonable price. The purpose of this plan is not to maintain a standard price. He believes that it is not appropriate to insert a clause stipulating that the entire issue should be reconsidered when the market price exceeds a certain limit. It is impossible to determine what is a reasonable price without considering the world situation and future costs. The members of the Management Committee are actually not appointed by the British government. The government believes that one of the groups representing the interests of consumers can represent the interests of British industry. Labor Party member Groves asked whether the governments of Malaya and Ceylon could be asked to appoint representatives of consumer interests to join the International Committee so that this plan would have harmonious cooperation from all parties. Colonial Secretary Lister replied no. This plan clearly stipulates that the industries concerned can state their opinions. (7th Reuters dispatch)

Nationality Issues After Foreign Women Marry Chinese Men 47

(Nanjing) Belgian Ambassador Ji Youmu inquired to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs about the situation where a Belgian woman married a Chinese man, but did not submit her marriage to the internal affairs for record. According to Chinese law, what should the woman's nationality be? The Ministry of Foreign Affairs consulted the Ministry of Internal Affairs for reply, saying that a foreign woman who marries a Chinese man acquires Chinese nationality according to the original text of the Nationality Law, but if she has not declared it to the Ministry for record, then the woman cannot be considered to have acquired Chinese nationality. As for whether she has lost her original nationality due to the marriage relationship, it depends on how the nationality law of her home country stipulates. (8th Special Dispatch)

Relief for Commercial Problems in Beijing 59

(Nanjing) Wang Chongzhi, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, said that the major loan for rescuing commerce in Beijing is still under study. It has been found that banks in Beijing, Shanghai, Jiangsu, and other places have already loaned out a total of seven to eight million yuan. From the perspective of the Beijing market, this amount is not small. With these millions, the circulation of the market is still allowed. However, the money market is still tight, and merchants are still hoping for loans. The reasons for this must be thoroughly investigated. Where has this cash gone, and why can't it circulate? If loans are needed, which industries need them most, and how much is needed? In short, banks take lending as their business, but for the sake of loan safety and rescue effectiveness, they have to be cautious. The Beijing Municipal Government is quite concerned about small businesses and is now planning to find ways to provide relief. Because the capital of the average small business is limited, and the market has been sluggish and business has been weak in recent years, most of their meager capital has been lost. If relief is not provided, the average vendor will have no way to make a living. Therefore, the Municipal Government decided to borrow one to two hundred thousand yuan from the bank and lend it to all small businesses in the city who need relief at low interest, with loan amounts ranging from fifty to one hundred yuan, so that the average small business can truly benefit. The loans will be implemented as soon as they are borrowed. (8th Special Dispatch)

Bai Yunti Talks About the Overall Situation in Mongolia: Bai Returns to Beiping from Bailingmiao; Changes in the Mongolian Race and the Ten Places 78

Beiping Communication: Bai Yunti arrived in Beiping on the 3rd after returning from Mongolia and is scheduled to leave Beiping for Nanjing within a few days. The reporter met with Bai yesterday. According to him, "After arriving in Beiping from Bailingmiao, I visited Chairman He at 3 pm yesterday, reported on the establishment of the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee, and urged him on behalf of the Mongolian people to take office as the Director of the Mongolian Autonomous Guidance. He has agreed to consult with the Central Government and the intention to resign is expected to be dispelled. I originally planned to leave Beiping for Nanjing tomorrow, but I still have official business to discuss with He, so the departure will be postponed. The Mongolian Political Affairs Committee is preparing to establish an office in Nanjing." Bai also spoke at length about the current situation of the Mongolian race, vividly and thoroughly, and recorded its main points as follows: "Mongolia was once a strong and great nation. Its race is distributed on the earth as far as Hungary, Romania, and Central Asia, Siberia, and the north and south of the Gobi Desert in Europe. Unfortunately, they are now mostly under the domination of foreign iron hooves. To the north of Outer Mongolia, that is, the large mountain on the east bank of Lake Baikal, there are about 500,000 Mongolians living there. Geographically, it is called "Buryat Mongolia." As early as the Kangxi and Yongzheng years of the early Qing Dynasty, when China and Russia delineated the border, due to the darkness of the Qing court's diplomats, the land and people north of the Kyakhta trade city were all given to Russia. The more than 2 million Mongolian people in Outer Mongolia are now also receiving assistance from Soviet Russia to train their troops, consolidate their national defense, educate their children, and build their roads in preparation for the outbreak of a Japanese-Russian incident, in which case they will take up arms and fight the Japanese. At present, the Kulun arsenal is in the hands of the Mongolian people, and the manufacturing of military supplies is extremely busy. There are currently 300 airplanes in Outer Mongolia. At the intersection of the Zhangku Highway and the Inner and Outer Mongolia border, a place called Ud, there are 50 fighter planes stationed there, all of which are Mongolian, in case of unforeseen circumstances. Heavy troops are gathered in the eastern part of Outer Mongolia to meet unexpected needs. The cavalry of Outer Mongolia has long been known in history. Once trained, it will be unparalleled in strength. Moreover, since the independence of Outer Mongolia, a conscription system has been adopted. The peacetime force may be too thin, but in the event of war, the whole country will immediately become soldiers. Therefore, it seems impossible for a strong neighbor to try to get involved in Outer Mongolia today. Since the Sino-Russian conflict caused by the Middle-East Railway Incident in 1929, Outer Mongolia has adopted a closed-door policy and set up checkpoints on its eastern, southern, and western borders, strictly prohibiting foreigners from entering. One of its purposes is to prevent the intrusion of Chinese merchants, so that the people of Outer Mongolia can use Russian goods as much as possible. As a result,

Prices in Outer Mongolia are soaring today. For example, one catty of pork is worth two yuan. Therefore, Mongolian-Chinese trade is really a matter that cannot be delayed any longer today. Outer Mongolia is currently adopting a gold standard system. Its currency unit is a silver coin weighing five qian, which is slightly lighter than the national currency. One and a half Mongolian yuan can be exchanged for one national yuan. At present, Mongolian banknotes can be seen circulating in Bailingmiao and other places. In addition to Russia, the government of Outer Mongolia also has a German embassy in Kulun. As for the situation in Inner Mongolia, the three eastern leagues have fallen to Japan. The Japanese road network in Rehe has been completed, and they plan to build a railway directly to Duolun and Chifeng, which are expected to be completed within the year. Their active military construction is really amazing. Everyone knows their desire for Ximeng. As for the news of setting up a radio station in Ximeng and operating in the three western leagues, they are all inaccurate. When I arrived at Bailingmiao, I did not see any Japanese people along the way. As for the matter of setting up a radio station in Ximeng, a radio station was once transported by car to request its establishment, which is true. After being rejected, the station was taken back, and there was no use of force to set up the station. As for the autonomy of western Inner Mongolia, if it is done step by step, it will indeed be a bright road. The work planned by the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee today is to first establish normal schools in each league as the basis for education. Secondly, actively carry out projects such as establishing woolen factories and developing the industry in southern Mongolia. The population of Inner Mongolia is 5 million. The population in the areas not occupied by the Japanese is about 2 million. Among them, about 50-60% are literate. If the domestic politics are clear and bright, all Mongolians are still willing to join the Republic of China to escape the oppression of foreign races. This depends entirely on whether our country has a solution in the future." (6th)

After the Southern Route Army Recaptures Junmenling, It Actively Handles Appeasement and Rehabilitation Work; Ye Jianying's Bandits Launch Two Counterattacks Without Success 79

Shantou Communication: The Southern Route Army recovered all the important passes of Junmenling on April 22. Li Yangjing inspected the front line on the 25th to handle the appeasement and rehabilitation work of Junmenling, recruit refugees to return to form anti-communist groups, and ordered all armies to rush to build highways connecting Pingyuan, Wuping, and Xunwu counties, with a deadline of completion before June. As for the Red bandits, after Ye Jianying retreated from Junmenling to Luotian Qingxi, they launched a fierce counterattack the next night. Zhu De and Peng Dehuai's bandits also assisted Ye from the two routes of Huichang and Ruijin. Peng Dehuai personally went to Luotian to supervise the battle. However, the defensive works of the Southern Route Army were extremely strong. The bandits attacked every night but were repelled. On the evening of the 26th, Peng and Ye's bandits attacked Junmen again with more than 10,000 troops. Huang Yanzhen's division also defended the dangerous areas. On the morning of the 27th, Li Yangjing received an urgent report from the front line and immediately transferred Huang Zhiwen's division to advance and assist. Luo Tangyan Yingyu's brigade continued to push up to Panggu Pass, and Zeng Youren's tribe advanced from Guikeng to the front of Luotang. At the same time, Chen Jitang telegraphed Wang Zanbin's division in Anyuan to detour to Tianxin and Longdong to attack the communist bandits from the side. Wang's divisions of Su Ling set out on the 29th and arrived at Junmenxu on the 30th to join the front-line operations. At that time, the army and bandits were still fighting fiercely near Junmen. Li Zhenliang and Deng Longguang's divisions were also preparing to join the front lines of Xunwu and Anyuan. The strength of each army was very strong, and the bandits ultimately failed. On the 29th, Li Yangjing convened a military meeting of the tribal chiefs of each division in Jitan. All the division commanders attended and decided that the 7th and 8th divisions would implement the Lianbao Law in accordance with the training and political guidelines for recovering the bandit areas, organize anti-communist groups, handle local autonomy, investigate households, number doorplates, and accept and rehabilitate bandits and communists who have reformed. All captured bandits and communists were transferred to the rear reformation院. At the same time, each regiment of each unit at the front was equipped with a radio station to facilitate military opportunities. According to reconnaissance reports, Zhu De, Lin Biao, Luo Binghui, Xiao Ke, Peng Dehuai and other bandits were divided into three army groups, with no less than tens of thousands of people, and were still trying to attack in full force. (May 1)

Xue Yue's Troops Capture Longgang in a Bloody Battle and Prepare for Another Major Advance to Directly Attack the Pseudo-Central Area 80

Nanchang Communication: Xue Yue's troops of the Sixth Route Army advanced from Yongfeng to Ningtou and Xingguo. In April, after clearing out the bandit nests in Shaxi and Shanggu in southern Yongfeng, they recovered Longgang, where the pseudo-county government was located, on the 26th. Longgang is located in the Yongfeng, Ji'an, Xingguo, and neighboring areas, adjacent to Donggu (i.e., Pingchi County) in the west, and parallel to Xiaopu Wangbei on the right. It is an important road to Xingguo and Ningtou, and the terrain is dangerous, so it is a must for strategists. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, it was once recovered, and then occupied by bandits again. The bandits used this place as a contact base for the junction of western, eastern, and southern Jiangxi, and built solid fortifications, which they valued very much. After Xue's troops captured Shaxi, about five or six thousand soldiers from various pseudo-independent divisions and independent regiments retreated here. In mid-April, a certain division used one brigade as the vanguard and one brigade as a reserve to rush towards Longgang. The pseudo-23rd Division and the pseudo-independent 1st and 2nd regiments were perched around Longgang, occupying dangerous fortress fortifications and stubbornly resisting. Ma's regiment first engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits. From morning to noon, they destroyed more than a dozen bandit fortresses in a row. Before long, they surrounded Longgangxu. Zhou's regiment took the opportunity to attack. Except for a part of the bandits who stubbornly defended the fortress on the large mountain in the south, the rest retreated. Ningtou was completely in the hands of the suppression army. However, the Nanshan fortress stood tall on the extremely high ridge of Fox Mountain, with cliffs on the left and deep valleys on the right, like a natural moat. A certain regiment used one battalion of troops to encircle the fortress and attack upwards, engaging in hand-to-hand combat more than a dozen times, but all failed. More than a dozen artillery shells were used, but they only broke a water tank used by the bandits to store water. The bandits took the opportunity to counterattack, and the soldiers of the suppression army became even more angry and climbed up at the risk of their lives, digging up landmines, destroying bamboo nails and deer fences, and removing obstacles. Dong Jintang, a sergeant of the 3rd company, and Liao Guoqing, a sergeant squad leader of the 6th company, crawled forward in a snake-like manner and rushed to the top of the fortress in the rain of bullets, aiming their bayonets and guarding the gate of the fortress. One of the pseudo-political commissars who was supervising the battle was killed on the spot. His comrades saw it and rushed up, and all the bandits in the fortress were captured alive. Longgang was finally settled. Currently, Xue Yue is actively handling the aftermath of Longgang and preparing to launch a major offensive towards Ningtou and Xingguo. Once Donggu Toubei Yuexi Liangcun is captured, the pseudo-central area can be suppressed from Xingning, and the bandits' interior can be penetrated.

(May 6)

Tragic Suicide of Mother and Daughter in Nanhui 81

A few days ago, a woman carrying an eight-year-old girl took a long-distance bus from Shanghai to Zhoupu, intending to hire a boat to the east gate of this county. Suddenly, she wanted to jump into the river to commit suicide at the Xuaidi Zhai in Tu 95 on the way. The boatman Lu Asheng stopped her and, accompanied by the clerk there, went to the Tanzhi Qiao Zhen police station. The police station then presented the woman, the girl, 190 yuan in cash, a term deposit certificate from the post office, and miscellaneous clothes to the Xinchang Public Security Fourth Branch for verification. According to the woman, her name was Xia Meiying, she was 32 years old, and her original籍 was Shaoxing. Her husband, Zhang Yunsheng, was from outside the east gate of this county. He used to be a detective in Shanghai. Now she came to the south from the Huilv Hospital on Aiwanyi Road, Beinicheng Bridge, Shanghai. When asked why she wanted to commit suicide, she said that her husband had embezzled money and drove her away, ignoring her alimony, and was addicted to smoking, so there was no hope for the future, so she did this. However, what she said did not seem to be true, and it was probably caused by deep nerve stimulation. The bureau ordered the police to send her to a Xinchang Hotel for temporary rest. The woman went to the bureau again the day before yesterday and claimed that she had a relative named Ren Liyuan who lived at No. 8 Ailin Lane, Xujiahui Road, Xieqiao, Shanghai, Hongyuanfa Stove, and another relative named Xie Dianrong who lived at No. 5 Jimao Lane, Nancang Street, Nanshi, Shanghai, and asked to send letters to inform them that they could solve the affairs of her and her husband, and said that she did not want to live in a hotel and asked to be sent to a nunnery for recuperation. The bureau entrusted someone to send her to the Hongmiao nunnery in Nanshi, the town. Unexpectedly, the woman suddenly used a sharp pair of scissors to cut off her daughter's throat and kill her at about 12 noon yesterday, and then committed suicide with the scissors. The situation was very tragic. The nun in charge of the nunnery, Hua Shengshi, immediately reported the incident to the bureau and then to the county government, requesting that someone be sent to examine the body.

Kunshan: Minsheng Company Suddenly Searched 82

The Minsheng Southern Goods Candy and Biscuit Company on Beida Street was opened with funds raised by Cantonese overseas Chinese, and the Cantonese Wu Zijing was appointed as the manager. Wu was stationed at the Minyou Store outside Ximen, Taicang. Since the company opened last autumn, business has not been very prosperous. At 1 pm on the 7th, County Magistrate Peng Baichuan suddenly received a secret report that the company was hiding red pills, opium, morphine, and other drugs. After receiving the report, Magistrate Peng immediately ordered Police Captain Luo Qixiang and Water Patrol Captain Yang Chunsheng to lead more than a dozen team members to search. For a time, crowds gathered and north-south traffic was blocked. The search lasted for three hours, but nothing was found and they left. When the team members went to the company to search, the company staff first checked the team members' bodies. Afterwards, the company staff immediately telegraphed Manager Wu and asked him to come to Kunshan as soon as possible. They also reported to the county chamber of commerce to investigate the reporter to the county government for negotiation.

Wuxi: Detective Team Captures Notorious Bandit 83

Zhong Jizhao, the captain of the detective team of the County Public Security Bureau, received a secret report that the notorious bandit Huang Zhenhu and Du A'er, who had committed many crimes, had come to the city from the countryside and were staying at the Dazhong Hotel to prepare to gather their old party and go to the countryside to commit crimes. After receiving the report, Zhong immediately sent officers to strictly guard against them. The day before yesterday, they went to the address to arrest them. Du came out to answer the door and was arrested by the police first. When Huang Zhenhu saw this, he immediately carried a rifle, opened the window, and tried to escape. Detective Wang Shuanglin also followed and jumped out of the window to chase him directly. Huang was finally arrested next to the barbed wire fence of the railway station, and the pistol was seized and taken to the team along with Du. According to Huang Zhenhu's confession, he was from Hushu Pass and had committed robbery at the house of a Du surnamed Hua in Houchang, Dang Kou, injuring the principal. Du A'er confessed that he was from Anzhen, this county, and worked in the countryside, following Huang to commit crimes in Dang Kou and shooting the principal. According to Zhong's confession, Chen Yuchu of the New Public Security Bureau had arrived in Xin yesterday, so he would hand over the case for verification.

Liu Zhuo's Case of Malfeasance in Office: No Prosecution 84

Liu Zhuomin, former Chief of the Second Public Security Bureau, was arrested and imprisoned for resisting the transfer of office and obstructing official duties, involving Li Shuyun, the mother and daughter of Gu Renfa, the former Commissioner of the Department of Civil Affairs of Jiangsu Province, causing a great uproar and a national sensation. The details have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. When Liu Zhuomin was in office, he was accused of bribing Zhang Keqin, a soil smuggler, with 770 yuan at 3:00 p.m. on January 25th of this year, and releasing him and 60 packages of opium. Ji Zaiyang handled the transaction, Liu Zhuomin received 600 yuan, and bureau member Sun Zhongjie received 170 yuan, etc. The prosecutor's office repeatedly summoned witnesses for interrogation. The investigation has now been completed, and it is believed that the evidence is insufficient. Chief Qian has decided not to prosecute.

Changzhou: Worker at Minfeng Cotton Mill Crushed to Death 85

The various construction matters of the Minfeng Cotton Mill outside Xiaonanmen, Wuyi County, have been contracted to Yang Hongji Construction Company of Shanghai, which sent workers to Changzhou. At around 7:00 a.m. on the 7th, Wu Jinxiang, a plastering foreman, was plastering the wall above the yarn-rocking room. There was a small machine pulley and belt above, which was running very slowly. Wu Jinxiang intended to step over the small pulley, but accidentally his clothes were caught in the belt. Suddenly, his whole body was pulled onto the pulley, and both his hands and feet were crushed. Others noticed and quickly stopped the machine, but Wu had already been tragically crushed to death. The person in charge of the factory heard the news and, in addition to telegraphing Yang Hongji Construction Company in Shanghai, reported the incident to the Second Public Security Bureau, which forwarded it to the County Prosecutor's Office to send personnel for an inquest. Prosecutor Guan Junjie led officials to the scene and confirmed that the death was due to crushing. The Shanghai factory sent someone to Changzhou to collect the body.

Wujiang: Head of Yanmu Beiyuan Township Kidnapped 86

Chen Tianxiang, the head of Beiyuan Township in Yanmu District of the county, comes from a family of modest wealth and has long been coveted by bandits. The night before last, a large group of more than a dozen bandits, all armed with guns, climbed over the wall and broke into his house. They rummaged through chests and boxes, stealing many clothes and ornaments. Before leaving, they also kidnapped Chen Tianxiang. Chen is already 63 years old, and his family is currently asking the county to pursue the bandits.

Taixian: Xiangtai Steamer Robbed by Bandits 87

The Xiangtai steamer of the Dadong Steamship Company of this county, which was sailing from Dongtai to Taixian, encountered more than 30 bandits at around 2:00 p.m. yesterday when it was passing near the north of Dongbiancheng. Each of them was holding a box gun and lurking in the important places on the bank, shouting to stop the boat and firing guns as a warning. Two boats were used to board the steamer and rob it clean. It is said that the loss was about 300 yuan in silver dollars.

Yangzhou: Notorious Bandit Gu Henglou Escorted to the Provincial Capital 88

Last year, the county government of this county dispatched a police team to Taixian to arrest a notorious bandit named Gu Henglou, and seized a box of red pills. He was interrogated and escorted by the team. Now, the provincial authorities, based on a secret report, said that Gu had bribed the county government with money, ordering Gu to be escorted to the provincial capital for disposal. After receiving the order, Magistrate Ma dispatched police team leader Zhu Xinke and squad leader Han on the morning of the 7th to escort Gu, along with the red pills, to the provincial capital for handling.

Silk Fabric Industry Faces More Disputes 89

The depression of the silk fabric industry in this county has reached its extreme. In addition, last year, Hangzhou merchants came to Yangzhou to organize Dasheng branches. Their competitive selling and chaotic behavior has become increasingly uncontrollable. The Silk Fabric Guild had previously petitioned various agencies to ban them, but the issue has not been fully resolved. Recently, Wang Heqing, seeing that the Hangzhou merchants were able to cause such disruption, also came to Yangzhou to speculate. He specially opened a new Xinji brand at the site of the bankrupt Hongxing store, selling silk and satin foreign goods at auction, which will inevitably cause disputes among competitors.

Zhenjiang: Industrial Bank Adds Branches 90

Since its opening, the Zhenjiang Industrial Bank has seen its business develop daily, especially with the most remittances from north of the Yangtze River. It has now been decided to establish branches in Taixing and Taizhou, north of the Yangtze River. Personnel have already been dispatched to prepare, and they are expected to open on the 15th of this month. It is said that President Bian of the Beijing branch has been transferred to Xiamen by the head office, and his vacancy will be filled by President Gu Bochun of the Zhenjiang branch, who will go to Beijing to replace him. The affairs of the Zhenjiang branch will be handled by Vice President Yan Zhongfan.

Danyang: Provincial Committee Inspects Police Corps in Danyang 91

The police team of this county was previously ordered by the province to reorganize into three detachments and one independent detachment. After that, it was required to be organized and established by May 1st, awaiting inspection by members of the Security Department. After receiving the order, Magistrate Bi completed the reorganization and reported it to the Provincial Security Department, which specially dispatched inspectors Liu Jingtan, Zhang Zhong, etc., to Danyang to assemble the county police team at the public sports field for inspection. The committee members have now gone to Jintan and other counties for inspection before coming to Danyang to inspect the defense corps.

Jiaxing Rickshaw Strike Causes Turmoil 92

The Jiaxing rickshaw pullers demanded a reduction in rickshaw rent. Although the party and government mediated, the company did not allow a daily reduction of five cents in rent, and still collected four dimes of silver dollar per day, resulting in a second strike by all rickshaw pullers starting on the 7th. On the 8th, the rickshaws were still not out. Gao Derun, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, specially went to Rufei Rickshaw Company in front of Xuanmiao Temple at 1:00 p.m. to persuade the rickshaw pullers to go out. However, some workers, because the rent reduction issue had not been resolved, prevented them from going out, resulting in a conflict between the two sides. They used iron tools to beat each other, and many rickshaws were destroyed. Rickshaw puller Chen A'da suffered head injuries from iron tools (caused by the shop assistants of Xinyang Ironware Store, which is adjacent to the rickshaw company). Lu A'rong, the owner of a nearby opium shop, was also beaten. Subsequently, the patrol team of the Public Security Bureau arrived and took Chen A'fa, the owner of Rufei Rickshaw Company, rickshaw pullers Ying Xianglian, Hu Jiangao, Wang Xiaolong, Chen A'da, Shen Jinkun, Zhou Ziwen, airport worker Xu Debiao, automobile worker Wang A'yi, and mechanics Chuan Lianggui and Lu Xingsheng, a total of eleven people, to the bureau and transferred them to the local branch court. Chen A'da was seriously injured and was carried to the court for examination. At 4:00 p.m., the Public Security Bureau summoned rickshaw puller representatives Deng Heyi and Chen Jinbiao to the bureau for reprimand. The government also summoned the rickshaw company owner for persuasion. Now the rickshaw company has softened and allowed a reduction of the rickshaw rent to 35 cents per day. The county government has issued a notice to the public, ordering the rickshaw company not to raise the rent and the rickshaw pullers not to instigate strikes, otherwise they will be arrested and dealt with. The matter has come to an end.

Hangzhou: Fire at New Market Injures People 93

At 7:30 p.m. on the 7th, a fire suddenly broke out at Daodexiang Sugar Food Store, No. 101 Yingzi Road, Hangzhou New Market. In an instant, thick smoke filled the air, and the fire broke through the roof. The fire brigade rushed to the scene to put out the fire, which was extinguished at 8:10 p.m. A total of four houses, including the Honglou Yindun Store and the Maoting Furniture Store, were burned, with a loss of about 10,000 yuan. When the fire was raging, Wang Yueyun, a partner of Yonghua Cloth Store at No. 99, was moving goods and was injured by an electric shock when a power line fell. Fortunately, he was rescued quickly and only injured his arm, with no danger to his life.

Local News: Today is National Humiliation Memorial Day, All Circles Hold a Grand Commemoration Meeting at 9:00 a.m. at the City Party Headquarters, All Entertainment and Banquets in the City are Suspended 94

Today is the 19th National Humiliation Memorial Day of Yuan Shikai's acceptance of Japan's unreasonable demands in the Twenty-One Demands.

The City Party Headquarters has scheduled a grand commemoration meeting at 9:00 a.m. today in the auditorium of the headquarters, convening representatives from all circles. Yesterday, special notices were sent to various agencies, groups, and schools, asking them to send representatives with letters to attend. A public notice was also issued. The Shanghai Municipal Police and the authorities, in view of the tense situation between China and Japan at this time, fear that some people will incite and disrupt public order. Strict precautions will be taken today.

Special notice is hereby given, hoping that all agencies, groups, schools, and party departments at all levels in this city will hold commemoration meetings separately, stop entertainment, and send two representatives with letters to participate in the Association's commemoration meeting. This is a matter of importance, and notice is hereby given."

Designated Meeting Staff 96

Separate Commemorations Held 97

Today is the National Humiliation Memorial Day, which is also one of the most painful pages in the history of national humiliation. The City Party Headquarters of this city believes that the central government stipulates that a mass meeting should be convened, but this port has special circumstances, so it has notified agencies, groups, schools, and party departments to send two representatives to the City Party Headquarters to participate in the commemoration meeting, and to hold separate commemoration ceremonies to be vigilant and to awaken the people's self-defense.

Yu Feipeng and Others Arrive in Shanghai, Military Transportation Inspection Group to Depart, Visiting Britain, France, Germany, Italy, Belgium, and Russia 98

The military transportation inspection group to Europe, organized by the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of Transportation, is scheduled to set sail on the Italian mail ship Conte Verde on the 11th. The entire group consists of 22 people, including Xu Tingyao as the head of the group, Yu Feipeng as the deputy head of the group, and Wei Yifu, Jiang Chu'ou, Si Lie, and Lu Hanqin as members of the group. Interview with the New Persian Consul 99

Advocating Direct Trade between China and Persia

Yesterday's Visit to Mayor Wu and Yu Ming

According to Xinsheng News Agency, Ostovan, the first Persian Consul General to China, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday afternoon. Yesterday afternoon, he visited Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng and Yu Ming, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In an interview with a reporter from Xinsheng News Agency at his residence in Cathay Hotel yesterday morning at 10:00 a.m., Mr. Ostovan said that Persia believes in Islam, but not all Persians believe in Islam, only the aristocracy and officials believe in it. I am also a Muslim. I am 45 years old and have been working in the Persian diplomatic service for 18 years. Before coming to Shanghai, I served as the consul in Karachi, India, for 32 months. This is my first time to China on this mission, and I admire the people, culture, etc. of China very much. I am very honored to have this opportunity to come to Shanghai. My position is that of a consul. In the future, other consuls may be appointed to Beijing, but I am only the consul in Shanghai.

Soon to Enter Beijing 100

Mr. Ostovan said that the establishment of the consulate is planned to be in the western district of the Public Concession. After finding a suitable location, I will enter Beijing to formally visit the diplomatic authorities of your country. The appointment of myself as the Persian Consul in Shanghai was discussed by the Persian Ambassador to Russia and the Chinese Ambassador to Russia. It is still awaiting the approval of the Nanjing government. After this approval is transferred from Moscow to the Persian government, I can enter Beijing to visit the diplomatic authorities.

Direct Trade 101

There are very few overseas Chinese in Persia, just like there are few Persian overseas Chinese in China. Persia's main imports to China and Persia's main exports to China are not direct imports and exports, and must be transshipped through other countries. Therefore, in order to promote commercial relations between China and Persia, it is necessary to have direct trade. For four hundred years, China and Persia have not sent formal representatives. The sudden dispatch of formal representatives this time is also due to this need, and it cannot be delayed any longer. As for the treaty relationship between China and Persia, a friendship treaty was concluded in Rome in 1920 by the ambassadors of the two countries stationed abroad. After that, it will be necessary to conclude a commercial treaty. As for whether I will be responsible for this negotiation in the future, or whether someone else will be appointed, it is up to the decision of the government authorities.

Recent Situation in Persia 102

Finally, Mr. Ostovan talked about the recent situation in Persia, saying that the Persian government changed on October 31, 1925. On December 13 of the same year, the new government was established, and it has been developing towards construction ever since. Persia is friendly to any country in the world. Persia's main products are many, such as oil, wool, felt, rice, silk, cotton, fruits, etc. The minerals include copper, iron, coal, lead, etc. The currency system used in Persia is also based on gold, named Pahlavi, just like the British gold pound and shilling. Each Pahlavi is equal to one hundred Birls, and each Birls is equal to one hundred Dinars.

Visiting Wu and Yu 103

When Mr. Ostovan was talking yesterday, he told reporters that he would visit Mayor Wu, Yu Ming, and US Consul General Cunningham. It is learned that Mr. Ostovan went to the Municipal Government to visit Mayor Wu at 3:00 p.m. yesterday, talking for about 20 minutes. Then, at 4:00 p.m., he went to the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Fenglin Bridge to visit Director Yu Ming, talking for about ten minutes, and then left. Mr. Ostovan suddenly refused to say whether he had visited US Consul Cunningham.

The Pope's Representative to China, Archbishop Zanin, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning, More Than 2,000 Catholics Welcomed Him at the Wharf, Staying in Shanghai for Two Weeks Before Going to Beijing to Meet Chairman Lin 104

Archbishop Zanin, the newly appointed Pope's representative to China, came to China by Italian ship on March 10. After arriving in Hong Kong, he went to various dioceses in South China for inspection. After completing his official duties, he took the Conte Verde from Hong Kong and arrived in Shanghai at 9:30 a.m. yesterday. The details of his arrival in Shanghai are recorded as follows:

2,000 Catholics Specially Welcome 105

The Conte Verde was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at about 6:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, but the ship was slower due to fog along the way, so it did not enter the port until 7:30 a.m. yesterday. At 8:30 a.m., it docked at Qichang Wharf. Local Catholics specially borrowed Zhengda Steamer from Datong Steamer Company to welcome him in advance. The Datong Wharf and the welcome special steamer were full of bright colors, and there were also colorful flowers tied into the words "Welcome Papal Envoy Archbishop Zanin". Those who took the special steamer to Qichang Wharf to welcome him included Monsignor Antongyi, Counselor of the Papal Representation in China, Fan Guozhu, Chief Secretary of the Papal Representation, Lu Bohong, President of the National Catholic Action Association, Bishop Zhu Kaimin of Haimen, Bishop of Zhejiang, Zhang Lu, President of Dongjiadu Academy, Li Ruokong, Zhao Shijing, more than 100 students from Zhengxiu First, Second and Third Schools, and military bands, etc. Together with those who welcomed him at Datong Wharf, there were more than 2,000 people.

Catholics' Audience with the Envoy: Solemn Etiquette 106

The special steamer departed from Datong Wharf at 8:00 a.m. and arrived at Qichang Wharf at 8:45 a.m. At that time, the Conte Verde had already docked, and Archbishop Zanin and his entourage stood on the deck. When the believers saw the envoy, they set off firecrackers and played military music. Archbishop Zanin did not board the special steamer until 9:00 a.m. Representatives of the believers stepped forward to pay their respects, presented flowers, and then walked into the ship's hall. Archbishop Zanin was supported to sit high in a red satin armchair, and the believers stepped forward to pay their respects and deliver welcome speeches for three or four minutes. Then they sat around for tea and snacks. At 9:30 a.m., they sailed back to Datong Wharf in Nanshi, landed, and took car No. 6500, escorted by the believers, directly to Bishop Hui's residence on Puxi Road, Xujiahui, to rest.

Archbishop Zanin's Past Experience 109

The newly appointed Papal Representative to China, Archbishop Zanin, is from Huierto, Venice Province, northern Italy. He was born on April 3, 1890. He entered the junior seminary of his diocese at a young age, and later entered the Belluno Major Seminary in his province to study theology. He then entered the Lecce National University to study philosophy and literature, and obtained a doctorate degree. On July 18, 1913, he was ordained as a priest in the Belluno Cathedral, and later became a pastor. He successively served as the supervisory pastor of the men's, women's, and youth departments of the Catholic Action Association, the deputy dean of the major seminary, and a theology professor. Six years later, he was transferred to be the bishop's secretary and was elected as the diocesan manager of the Papal, Propagation of the Faith Business Association. From 1922 to 1926, he served as a municipal consultant, assisting in the work of charitable organizations, orphanages, and empty shelters. He has the honorific title of "Father of the Poor". In 1930, he was promoted to the general secretary of the Pontifical Society of St. Peter the Apostle and was awarded the honorary title of bishop. On December 4 of last year, he was promoted to the second Papal Representative to China and set off for China on March 6.

Meeting Chairman Lin Two Weeks Later 110

According to Monsignor Antongyi, Counselor of the Papal Representation in China, who spoke to the Central News Agency reporter on the ship, Archbishop Zanin plans to stay in Shanghai for two weeks, and then go to Beijing to meet Chairman Lin of the National Government and the ministers of various ministries. Then, he will go to the Yangtze River area to inspect the church affairs of various dioceses. Once the inspection is completed, he will go to Peiping to reside. It is also learned that when Archbishop Zanin inspected church affairs in various places in South China, he believed that the church affairs in South China were handled very well, and the future teaching policy will still be carried out according to the original plan.

China General Chamber of Industry and Commerce Submits to the Ministry to Stabilize Prices 111

Set Minimum Price Based on Current Price of Raw Material Wheat

Regarding the issue of stabilizing the market price of flour, the China General Chamber of Industry and Commerce and the Shanghai Flour Industry Association previously submitted a request to the government, proposing urgent steps be taken within a short period of time to stabilize flour prices and relieve the rural areas. After the Ministry accepted the request of the two associations, Liang Shangdong, of the Department of Commerce, was dispatched to Shanghai on the 4th of this month to invite manufacturers to talk. However, their expression was not very clear, so the price of flour plummeted again on the 7th of this month, with a difference of more than a dime before and after, creating an extremely bad environment. The China General Chamber of Industry and Commerce, in view of the principle of stabilization, must be announced within a short period of time, so it once again requested the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for relief yesterday, stating its position and explaining the purpose of setting the minimum flour price. Both the theory and the facts are very sufficient. The principles of setting the minimum flour price that it advocates are recorded below. Regarding the issue of stabilizing the flour price, the association has submitted requests to the Ministry one after another. First, adopt the method used by the US government in 1933 to ban the New York Stock Exchange, first stop the exchange's bidding, so that various securities can gradually return to their original value during this period of suspension. According to the investigation, although the time is temporary, the effect is very significant. However, it is deeply concerned that once this step is implemented, it will inevitably cause other changes in the settlement price in the future, which will make the situation more confusing and lead to more disputes. After research and consideration by most experts, it is agreed that the government's power should be used to set the minimum price based on the current price of raw material wheat, which is relatively stable and easy to implement. Considering the current situation of flour prices, the degree and state of the price drop are not due to any drastic changes in a certain period of time, but a downward trend day by day and hour by hour. Therefore, once the minimum price is determined, it can at least have a considerable effect in the short term. The predicted results are analyzed as follows: (1) The current flour market customers are buying low because the Chinese economy is depressed and the prices of various goods are falling. Considering flour, it is in the same situation, so they only buy short and do not buy long, and over time, it has become a trend of gradual decline. Now, if there is a minimum price limit, it means that the government is expressing its determination to maintain flour prices and at the same time showing its clear behavior and trend. Then, customers will see that it is useless to sell short and will naturally buy low and buy high. For example, on April 27 of this year, the flour market had entered the two-yuan mark. Later, as news of government maintenance continued to spread, the market price gradually rose. By May 5, it had reached as high as two yuan and four cents. However, on the 6th, when the government representative returned to Beijing, it was reported that no definite solution had been reached, so the price plummeted again in one day on the 7th. Comparing the market prices before and after, there is a difference of more than a dime. This is enough to show that the rise and fall of the market price still depend on the market. If there is a force in the middle that can raise the price, it can of course have an effect in the short term. (2) The method of limiting the minimum market price is commonly used by governments in exchanges. Its effect can make the general public change their mentality and change from buying low to buying high. This method can not only increase the number of transactions in the exchange, but also enable the raw material merchants to extend their breathing power and buy a large amount of raw materials, so as to wait for a high price to sell. On the contrary, in the current situation, the flour price is gradually declining day by day, and the grain merchants dare not buy more wheat. However, if the flour price is predicted, no matter what, the flour price will never fall below a certain number, then more wheat can be imported at that time, and flour merchants can also import more flour. The transformation of the environment is that today's buying low is tomorrow's buying more. With the multiplication and evolution, the flour price can immediately go upward. This is the so-called use of the market's buying and selling opportunities to make the price of goods naturally stable.

Merchant Ships: Passenger Overload Prohibited - New Regulations Issued by the Ministry Now in Effect - Navigation Bureau and Customs Cooperate in Inspection 112

Ship overloading is most likely to cause accidents. Therefore, regarding restrictions on cargo loading, the Ministry has hired experts to establish a load line method. Similarly, excessive passenger loading also poses significant risks. Recently, the Inspector General of Customs petitioned the Ministry of Finance regarding the difficulty Customs faces in managing passenger overloads on Chinese vessels. The Ministry of Finance has consulted with the Ministry of Transportation and Communications and agreed to strictly enforce regulations when navigation authorities issue passenger capacity certificates for inland river vessels. However, because the Navigation Bureau currently only handles inspection, measurement, and registration matters, the issuance of permits and inspection of vessels entering and leaving ports has not yet been implemented. The Customs and Navigation Bureau are now closely cooperating to facilitate their duties, and the Ministry of Transportation and Communications has added new measures: (1) Hereafter, when issuing passenger capacity certificates, the navigation authorities should carefully assess the vessel's hull, machinery, boiler structure, and capabilities to ensure they meet minimum standards. Inspection certificates may be withheld if life-saving equipment is lacking. (2) Passenger-carrying vessels passing through Customs should present their vessel inspection certificate and passenger capacity certificate. If they lack these certificates or if Customs discovers that the number of passengers exceeds the allowed limit, the ship may be detained, and the nearby navigation authorities should be notified for punishment. (3) If, during departure or while en route, military personnel forcibly board a vessel, causing it to exceed its passenger limit, the captain or ship's officers should refuse them. If they are unable to resist due to force, they should report the incident to the local Customs office or the Customs office at the vessel's initial port of call, awaiting further instructions. The above three measures have been communicated to the Ministry of Finance, requesting that they be forwarded to all Customs offices, notifying all shipping companies to comply. After the promulgation of these new measures, the Customs and Navigation Bureau have been jointly conducting strict inspections of passengers on all vessels. Any vessel found to be overloaded will be immediately detained and punished. The Navigation Bureau has already instructed all shipping companies to report the number of passenger seats on each vessel for record-keeping purposes.

Conducting Through Transportation 121

Ports on the Sichuan River 122

Through Transportation Schedule 123

As for the through transport ticket prices for each port, they have all been set and will be published after printing.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables the Ministry of Finance - Requesting Extension of the Validity Period for Domestic Seafood Permits 124

Please Change Everything to One Year

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "According to a letter from the Shanghai Seafood and Grocery Industry Guild, a member, stating that the Changdexin, Maohe, and Dingyu Yuchang companies, also members, are engaged in domestic goods such as dried clams, wood ear, and shiitake mushrooms. When these goods are shipped from the place of origin to Shanghai, customs duties are paid and a permit is obtained for sale. The validity period is stipulated to be only six months, and the validity period of the dried shrimp permit is also only eight months. If the stock is not sold out within these six or eight months, it must be taxed again if it is to be transferred to other ports. Moreover, the standard of taxation is estimated at market price, which is twice the market price. Moreover, due to the ambiguity of valuation, there are often various difficulties in detention and punishment or tax supplementation. Then, not only are there overlapping tariffs, but also unexpected losses in valuation, which is unbearable and extremely painful. However, the import validity period of the same foreign goods is one year, and within one year, they can be transported and sold without any burden of overlapping taxation and unexpected valuation, so merchants with less capital and a heavy profit-making heart are more willing to promote foreign goods. Patriotic merchants are unexpectedly destroyed, which seems to be contrary to the government's policy of maintaining domestic production. It is reasonable to report the situation to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which will forward it to the Ministry of Finance, requesting the customs regulations. The validity period of the above permit should be changed to one year in order to relieve the burden and revive the merchants' difficulties." The association pointed out that "annual leakage is alarming." The reasons are nothing more than the fact that the people are extravagant in foreign goods, the national production is backward, and the merchants are only interested in profits and are happy to promote foreign goods, which is also quite relevant. Now that the government is maintaining domestic goods and promoting production to save the crisis, it seems that the validity period of the customs permit should be revised to one year in order to maintain the sales of domestic products. It is appropriate to report the situation and request the ministry to review and approve it as requested, which would be publicly appreciated. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully stated that the validity period of the domestic seafood and grocery import permit is only six months, and at most only eight months. After the deadline, the tax must be re-evaluated and taxed. Compared with the one-year foreign permit, the treatment is inevitably very different, and it is inevitable that merchants will tend to favor foreign goods. The industry association's request that the validity period of the domestic seafood and grocery import permit be changed to one year is a legitimate reason, and it is appropriate to report the situation. We respectfully request your ministry's review and approval, and request that the customs be ordered to comply with the processing, which would be publicly appreciated."

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Government passed the Regulations on the Examination of Traditional Chinese Medicine, a small number of doctors have requested the provincial government to exempt them from the examination. Yesterday (the 8th), it sent a cable to the Jiangsu Provincial Government requesting immediate implementation. The original cable stated (above omitted), "Chinese medicine has the deepest essence, and after thousands of years of social experience, the wise have elucidated it, and it does have considerable treatment skills. However, since the Republic of China, the government has taken a hands-off attitude towards traditional Chinese medicine, exiled in a state of self-reliance and self-destruction in an anarchic state. Therefore, there is no control over practice, and anyone can be a doctor. Pharmacy shop partners, itinerant drug dealers, and transformed Confucian doctors and family doctors, etc., have copied one or two common prescriptions, and have obtained a few jingles, and can hang a pot to save the world, using patients as experimental products. The prestige of medicine has fallen, and the lives of the people have suffered a great deal. The average mortality rate of Jiangsu population accounts for more than 30 per thousand, and this alarming super-high mortality rate, the rampant quack doctors, is the biggest reason. Premature death and ethnic vitality are destroying the social economy, and there is nothing worse than this. At present, there are more than 10,000 quack doctors in Jiangsu province in addition to good doctors. If the examination is not started immediately and prohibited from being produced, it will increase day by day and cause more harm. The regulations on the examination of traditional Chinese medicine, which were previously passed by the provincial government, are indeed tools to eliminate quack doctors and select outstanding ones. We sincerely request immediate implementation to save the people of Jiangsu and improve the status of traditional Chinese medicine. It is a virtue to say so."

In order to facilitate the people of this port to visit the scenic spots of Hangzhou, the Jinghu Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration has added a special express train for the weekend tour to Hangzhou. It was originally scheduled to depart from Shanghai North Station at 12:35 PM every Saturday afternoon. Gu Genfa, a local from Shanghai who lives at 151 Pushi Road in the French Concession and runs a car business, is 40 years old this year, and his wife, Zhang, is 39 years old this year. However, Cao knew that he had committed numerous crimes and was full of evil, and there was no way to escape the crime. Fortunately, the guard found it and took the knife. The injuries were still light, so he reported to the head of the police and sent Cao to Guangci Hospital for treatment. A Rhyming Dictionary Based on Yiyin Suozi is Published 141

Chinese characters have been developed through the six writing principles, and it is already very difficult to arrange and check them. However, if there are only questions about the pronunciation and meaning of a character, there are still books such as the Shuowen Jiezi dictionary and the Ciyuan dictionary that can be used to check and clarify them. Moreover, in recent years, there have been many people who have studied character retrieval, and the method of searching for characters by form is expected to be improved in the future. However, people often encounter the embarrassment of forgetting how to write a character when picking up a pen, so that even if they can say it, they cannot write it out, and there are almost no books that can be used for reference. Li Bingwei of Deyou Girls' School in Beiping, in view of this, gathered 20 to 30 colleagues to study and find a way to solve this difficulty. After spending seven years, they have now compiled a rhyming dictionary, which has been published. The content of the book is based on the order of the phonetic alphabet and the four tones, arranging the order of more than 20,000 Chinese characters, and the annotations are very clear and concise. Anyone who knows the phonetic alphabet can use it to check any character whose writing is unclear. Even those who are illiterate, if they know the phonetic alphabet, can check the writing of any character by themselves. It is truly an excellent tool for unifying the national language and popularizing literacy. Whether or not Chinese people are literate, they all need to purchase this book. The book is divided into two types: Chinese binding and Western binding, exquisitely printed on rice paper, and priced at three yuan. The reduced version is even cheaper, priced at only eight jiao or one yuan and several jiao. Ma Guotong Minshe outside Donghua Gate in Beiping is publishing it, and all major bookstores in various cities are selling it.
