Free Talk

Announcement from Li Liewen 218

Due to my current workload, I am unable to handle the editorial affairs of this publication. From today onwards, all matters related to this publication will be managed by Mr. Zhang Zisheng.

Ducks 219

— Miao Chongqun

One of Nanjing Cartoons

For a long time, the wild rice stem, water shield soup, and sea bass have been famous. I'm afraid that it's not only the famous scholars in Wu region who want them. If people with a slightly stronger appetite see these words, they may secretly smack their lips a few times and quietly swallow their saliva into their throats. After all, things in books cannot relieve hunger, just as saying that quenching thirst with plums is also a rhetorical statement. However, this era is different from the past. Things with some local flavor can almost arrive from morning till night, thanks to the convenience of transportation. For example, the Jiang leg from some place in Zhejiang has spread all over the country without promotion; also, the so-called "official gift" – ducks – from Nanjing have been brought to all directions as if they had been canonized.

As soon as you see a reed bag with the words "official gift" on it, you know it is Nanjing's duck. The Nanjing I know is almost the same as the era when I knew the official gift duck. So I think, oh Nanjing, the city of ducks!

The first time I went to a friend's house in Nanjing for dinner, there were four dishes on the table, and two of them were ducks, one red and one white, and I clearly saw that each piece of duck had clusters of black hair. I don't know why goosebumps appeared all over my body, and I secretly cried out in my heart - "Don't be polite, eat, it's the famous Nanjing duck." My friend kept putting duck pieces on my plate.

I chewed slowly, but besides tasting the inherent smell of duck, I didn't find any special "Nanjing" taste in the duck.

Bathing in the smell of duck, I couldn't eat more than half a bowl of rice. My bowl was full of duck, and my friend kept urging me:

"Eat duck!"

I thought to myself, is duck supposed to be a meal? But my friend's attitude seemed to tacitly agree. At the same time, he felt that I didn't understand the good intentions of the Nanjing people, and he looked a little unhappy. So he turned around and introduced the duck again:

"This red one is roasted duck; that white one is salted duck (pointing to the white one); it's even better in the autumn, there's also osmanthus duck..."

"Isn't there also official gift duck?" I interrupted him, but also supplemented his words.

"That's right, that's pressed duck."

This was the first time I learned about the names of Nanjing's ducks. Later, in a student's test paper (the topic I gave was probably "My Memories"), she described truthfully, roughly saying:

"... Usually I don't like to study hard, but when it came time to take the middle school entrance exam, I often worried and cried. My mother said it's okay, she would buy me duck to eat after I studied hard... Day after day passed, the food was very delicious, because every meal had my favorite dish - duck... The exam also passed, and the results were announced. Many friends were at my house that day. I passed the exam. My father walked in from outside, slapped the table and said loudly - he was ordering my mother, "Buy her more duck to eat!" At first, I was startled, but later I realized that it was to reward..."

Ducks in memory!

I often cursed the duck. I remember several times when I went out at dusk, I couldn't pass the entrance of the duck shop, countless people holding empty bowls waiting to cut the duck, densely packed the roads in the small alley. Because of the duck, I also cursed Nanjing. But when I thought of these people's love for the duck, their respect for the duck; when I thought of that time when I had dinner at my friend's house, I severely regretted that I had rejected my friend's kindness.

A Nanjing woman is now living with me. Sometimes when we quarreled, her annoying voice made me sigh silently; sometimes when I was angry, her kind of inspiring me... That day, the duck was so delicious! Even if I ate it all, it still wasn't enough... But later, many classmates said when they met, "Buying duck for you to eat!" My face turned red and white... In the blood of every Nanjing person?" But I didn't dare to say that.

It's not my speculation. From many, many aspects of understanding, I gradually knew that Nanjing's duck is not only diverse in name, but the duck does have a kind of "mysterious", "exciting" power in Nanjing. Where is it? "Lurking in the sickening qualities, again made me sigh in silence. But seeking peace is also quite easy. As long as you propose to buy duck to eat, then everything is over. However, I never said anything that would replace my sigh; I can't say, "You duck-like throat and qualities."

Ducks are probably the most, most numerous slaughter in Nanjing; but I don't know on what person or blood the countless "duck spirits" are entrusted.

On Reform 220

— Sanxin

If "the rise and fall of the world is the responsibility of every individual" is not the ramblings of a madman but must be taken as one's own guide, then one should pay a little attention to the methods of implementing this responsibility!

Perhaps this is not too demanding. When reforming society, one must first "abandon oneself." There are many people who attack others for personal grievances under the guise of reforming society, and there are also many people who rashly extend their own good experiences to others and introduce them to others. There are too many examples of the former "using public office for private gain", so there is no need to cite them; the latter is like "recommending a good doctor" or promoting Chinese medicine because it cured a minor headache, or advocating that everyone in the world should be vegetarian because oneself is vegetarian.

So, treating the times and helping the world is like a good doctor using medicine. Taking the patient as the main body, the method of diagnosis is worth considering. A certain Mr. once advocated opening up air circulation in houses as a way to demolish walls, but the result was just opening windows, but it was still the original purpose; this is a bitter word after understanding the method of reforming society. To reform such a huge and dark force at present, it cannot be done lightly and easily, but must be done with a grand strategy.

If a society is reformed without self, there is no reason why society should not be reformed. Aren't the Great Wall of China and the pyramids both man-made? Even the Heavenly Emperor is afraid of Yu Gong moving mountains. Moreover, when society has reached this point, everyone is thinking about reform, and everywhere can be reformed! It is not too much to use the method of overcorrection, even knowing that it is excessive. Three strikes at the Confucius shop in front, and then present a book of Analects (a magazine) for people to see, perhaps one can slightly tear off the paper crown of morality. This is just a small example, it is one method. Aiming at the weakness of society and throwing a spear is also a method. In addition, there are many feasible methods!

What is worrying is that oneself is "fair", sometimes not seeing the opponent's cruelty; only seeing the graceful smiling face, not seeing the true shape of their fangs and claws, at the moment when the enemy seems to be suing for peace and one is thinking of accepting their surrender, in fact one is surrounded!…

Enlightenment Movement 221

— Mu Mutian

A few days ago, I talked with a friend about the need for an enlightenment movement in China today. Another person said it was unnecessary. Does China really need an enlightenment movement now?

There is no need for high-sounding arguments, let us just look at the facts of China today.

We clearly know that there are literary critics today who do not know what "Don Quixote" is, and even more who do not know that Gorky is both a realist and a romantic writer. And this kind of person is a specialist, or a quasi-specialist, or a self-proclaimed specialist, and I'm afraid there is more than one.

Has Chinese literature entered a new stage? Of course, there are some good buds. But everywhere is still full of ignorance.

China is indeed an "old empire". Is it true that some men of letters and scholars are still living a medieval life in terms of knowledge?

During the "May Fourth" era, I went to Japan to study. A certain compatriot of mine was majoring in economics at the Imperial University. Someone advised him to read "New Youth". He said it was a Christian propaganda product and he would not read it.

Once, my friend Feng Junpei told me an interesting story. He said: A certain provincial supervisor went to the countryside to inspect schools. When he arrived at a certain middle school, he listened to the geography teacher teach geography. When he got to England, the teacher said, "England, 'England', the word 'Jili' is incomprehensible."

I also heard a middle school history teacher talk about Napoleon.

Are You Escaping? 222

Friend, do you want to escape in the dark night?

The shadows of demons are looming in front, the steps of ghosts are rumbling behind,

Forever and ever, panic will occupy your heart!

Escape, let you escape in the dark night!

Crossing the eerie canyon, listening to the howling of the forest?

The dark night is still in front of you, have you ever escaped the black net?

Gather your courage, poor thing!

You are not the only one walking in the dark night,

If you have courage, aren't the torches in front and behind?

Ming Dynasty Letters 223

— Shu

One

"Ming Dynasty Letters," in four volumes, compiled by Qing Dynasty scholars Wang Yuanxun Hanzhang and Cheng Hua in collaboration, based on the original Biyunlou edition. It collects letters from one hundred and sixteen figures, totaling three hundred and forty-six letters. The book includes a preface written by Wang Yi in the Mid-Autumn of the Yiyou year of the Kangxi reign, which begins by stating, "Letter writing is a minor skill, yet it cannot be done without mastery of the ancients." He then says, "Since the late Ming Dynasty, there have been dozens of compilers, but good editions are extremely rare." He criticizes Yang Yongxiu and Wang Pizhen's "Qingcai" anthology, saying, "It is regrettable that they are broad but not precise, incorporating the rhetoric of Zuo Qiuming, the edicts of the two capitals, which is out of place." Finally, he concludes that the two compilers "recognized the desolation of this field and sought to revitalize it, collecting the works of Ming worthies into one compilation, with meticulous selection and a genuine desire to avoid simply pleasing the masses." In reality, although this collection contains many fine pieces and the selection is careful, some parts are still inevitably lengthy and pedantic, inducing drowsiness, and its achievement is not significantly higher than "Qingcai." Typically, each person has one or two pieces included, at most five or six, while Zhang Juzheng has twenty-five specially selected, Gui Youguang fourteen, Tang Xianzu fifteen, Wang Heng fourteen, and Qian Qianyi fourteen, which clearly shows the compilers' preferences. The entire book is divided into four volumes, with short biographies preceding each letter, and the printing quality is excellent, with each person written and printed on a separate page in elegant calligraphy. To my knowledge, there is also a Suzhou edition, but the printing quality is far inferior to the original edition.

This book contains many lyrical works, and among them, the most sincere and poignant expression of the authors' emotions is represented by Zhonglang's letter "To Xiao Yunsheng, Libationer." This letter does not appear to be included in Zhonglang's collected works. The text reads: "The evening moon at Shetang, the spring willows at the West Gate, do you still remember our days together? Counting the years, in the past decade, old friends have dwindled, like morning stars. On Bo Xiu's grave, the poplars are almost thick enough to be pillars. How can one's thoughts not turn to ashes?" And Gui Youguang's letter to Shen Jingfu states: "Poetry is but weeping, it cannot be poetry. Yesterday I saw many friends who wanted to relieve my sorrow. The bond between father and son is gone! These tears are only for my son, and yet you want me to restrain myself?" The author's emotions are more explosive, and the turmoil of his mind can be seen between the lines. Regarding the expression of indignation, I found in this book Yang Shen's letter to Zhang Zhang: "In recent years, all thoughts have turned to ashes, only the habit of writing remains, which has burdened me and brought me trouble. Therefore, I boldly wrote on the wall: 'Old age and sickness make it difficult to approach pen and ink; I vow before the gods not to write poetry or prose.' From now on, I will live like a monk at home, with a bowl of porridge in the morning and a lamp in the evening. What I hold is Pang Gong's four words 'emptying all possessions'!" The author's misanthropic sentiments overflow the page, and his helpless escape is fully expressed. Furthermore, there is Fan Jingwen's letter to Huang Shizhai: "Since you left, the state of affairs has become unspeakable! Today is not yesterday, and I fear that next year will be even worse than this year! This hall is not a place for sparrows to dwell, and I am eager to return home. But the entire court is filled with mutual villagers, and the sovereign is isolated and helpless. I cannot bear to leave the country indifferently. I know that eating without contributing is useless, but I fear that if something happens, even someone to eat without contributing will not be found! This I say with tears!" His heartfelt indignation and contradiction are also fully revealed on the page.

"Please Instruct Me on Two Poems," With a Preface 224

— Tan Mi

Old Man Zhitang composed a poem for his fiftieth birthday. Famous figures from all over the country wrote poems in response. In particular, a couplet from a certain gentleman, "The edge of the trousers sweeps the ground, suspected of a sick horse," can be described as uniquely brilliant. In addition, "Tea is bitter because it is bitter tea" can also be considered a wise saying. Mi is also fond of poetry, and I respectfully offer two poems in rhyme to Mr. Lin for his amusement.

"Academic Scoundrel" Sir is also from a distinguished family, Stirring up mud and soil on the monk's robe.

The mischievous child once taught the startled crane to cry, The blaring speaker now transforms into a soaring serpent.

Idly watching the Shanghai school flow like water, Hearing that the world is as chaotic as hemp.

Peach and plum blossoms are in full bloom, spring is just right, It doesn't hurt to brew tea slowly under the flowers. (Note 1)

"Humorous" like you, quite the "master," Casually blowing smoke and mist around the monastic robe.

The human world is originally full of mice, And the Master has always hated lazy snakes.

There are many small pieces, like snail tracks on the wall, But the great sound is helpless against the tortoise shell playing hemp. (Note 2)

The high hill has no leftover pieces, Another cup of tea stirs up trouble.

(Note 1) Jinggong has the line "When watching flowers in Jin Valley, don't casually brew tea."

(Note 2) The Tang people have the line "Paper repairs the zither, hemp joins the strings."

. Guess what he said? He said, Napoleon, his strength is like an ox, he can break the wheels of a car, hence the name Napoleon.

Facts of this kind are innumerable. But these are things of the past. What about now? Now, let's look at our middle schools. Of course, some schools are writing eight-legged essays in vernacular, but there are probably quite a few that are still writing classical Chinese essays on "Love of Country," "On Emperor Gaozu of Han," "On the Origin of Man," and so on.

Now, the completion of the railway network in "Manchukuo" and the construction of Rajin Port to complete the shortest route between Japan, Korea, and Manchuria are probably still unknown to most Chinese people. It seems not at all strange that university graduates do not know where Chifeng is.

In all aspects, it is revealed that Chinese people lack common sense. It seems that the field of literature and art cannot be an exception. In China today, there are very few people who have a general idea of world literature. We are still in the age of the omnipotent noun. One glance reveals young people in Western clothes, spouting new nouns and new terms, but it is highly questionable whether they have a deep understanding of any particular thing.

I believe that we should carry out a thorough enlightenment movement for young literary people. From all aspects, from shallow to deep, we should make them truly understand literature and art. Compared with writers and critics in advanced countries, our critics and writers are, to put it bluntly, much more naive. I believe that everyone should carry out a thorough, enlightening educational endeavor for themselves. Are our critics and writers mostly suffering from naivete?

I believe that an enlightenment movement is very necessary now. Don't you think so?

Shanpu Lottery Ticket (4) 225

— Tang Xiru

In this stillness, suddenly a car, like a fat pig in a hurry, howled a few times and rushed past A-Fa, sweeping a cloud of dust onto him.

"Don't be so smug! In three days, I'll buy one for you to see!" As he thought this, he not only didn't resent the car that had just passed, but he laughed.

Three days later... He really hoped that tomorrow would be three days later!

(Three)

The third day, which seemed like it would never come, finally arrived and passed.

A-Fa didn't win. Although this was a year of miracles, there were still many things that would disappoint you.

But wait, God blesses those who are patient and willing to wait.

Of course, after failing, A-Fa couldn't help but blame himself, mocking himself. His wife and children were starving in the countryside, and he was being absurd here! How difficult it was to circle ten out of one hundred and twenty characters and get seven right! Two jiao was not a small amount, enough for him to eat two or three meals! If he was going to be absurd, he might as well go to the Guangdong Theater to see the "Female Knight-Errant of the Wasteland River," which would be more worthwhile! ...

There were not a few reasons for his self-reproach, and the reasons were not insufficient. But everything was in vain, unable to stop the desire to get rich. This failure strengthened his determination to buy a Shanpu lottery ticket even more. If he didn't buy it, the two mao he lost last time would have to be considered a total loss, and he wouldn't be able to recoup it, which he was unwilling to accept. Moreover, with one hundred and twenty characters, how much could they vary? Surely they would come out one day! He didn't believe it, he insisted on betting on these characters!

He had already bought Shanpu tickets, and it was not difficult to walk into the Xinglong lottery shop. He bought his second ticket.

Again, anxious waiting, fearful waiting; again, many fantasies, beautiful soap bubble-like fantasies.

Silk and Tea, Spring Silkworm Season in Full Swing 246

(Hang County) This year's sericulture in the four townships of Hang County is purely affected by unfavorable weather. Although the instructors have tried their best to adjust the temperature and humidity and carefully raise the improved varieties bred in Linping, Gaosi, Sanbao, Hushu, Xiecun, and other places, the silkworms repeatedly experienced eye loss and leaf retention after the second sleep. The local silkworm varieties raised in the remaining areas of the upper four townships have shown signs of white stiffness and diarrhea in the second and third stages, resulting in significant losses. Fortunately, the weather has now turned sunny and warm, with early batches already reaching the large-eye leaf-opening stage, and late batches also reaching the three-eye leaf-foot stage, and development is improving.

(Fuyang) This year, farmers, aware of the unfavorable silkworm breeding in recent years, have weak ant breeding this year, and many are breeding local varieties. The weather is cold, and ant collection is late. The development of improved varieties is also slow. After leaf opening, the humidity is high and the temperature is low, and local silkworms repeatedly experience problems, with yellowing, black vomiting, and losses of 40-50%. Currently, the early batches in Dayuan Town, Tangjiabu, and other places have reached the three-eye leaf-foot stage. The late batches of improved silkworms in Shuxi and other areas are only at the three-eye robust leaf stage. In the past two days, the weather has been sunny and warm, and silkworms have developed smoothly and eaten leaves vigorously.

(Chongde) This year's silkworm season in various townships has been severely damaged due to continuous rain and cold weather. Improved silkworms have not developed well. Improved varieties are mostly bred in Tujia Dam and Fujia Bridge, so the silkworm season is later. Rural economies in Shimenwan, Wuhejing, Taizitang Bridge, and other places are declining, and local silkworm varieties are bred, resulting in heavier losses. Fortunately, the weather has now turned sunny and warm, and the temperature has risen sharply. The silkworms' development is improving, with early batches having opened leaves for three or four days after the second sleep, and late batches also having sufficient leaves. The current situation is quite good.

The Arms Race Among the Great Powers and the Second World War 250

By Jia Wei

Recent newspapers are truly frightening. The date of the "General Disarmament Commission" on May 30th is approaching day by day, but unexpectedly, every day carries headlines such as "General Disarmament Almost Hopeless, European Countries Anxious and Insecure," "World War Clouds Loom, Arms Factories in Various Countries Busy Manufacturing Weapons," "British Insurers Refuse to Underwrite War Risk Insurance," "War Rumors in Europe Intensify," "France Decides to Expand Navy," "Greed of Eastern Neighbors Unquenchable, Soviet Chairman Inspects National Defense," "Situation in the Far East Shifts, US Navy Expansion Imminent"... Using large fonts and bold statements is truly shocking. At the same time, let's look at some recent, and perhaps already past (because this is "increasing day by day") "small statistics": the world's annual military expenditure reaches 500 million gold yuan; Germany's military budget this year increased by more than 40% compared to last year; Japan's naval construction has already reached 95% of the treaty limit; France's military expenditure accounts for 20% of its budget, with each French person bearing an average military expenditure of 13.6 US dollars, the highest in the world... In this way, the so-called effectiveness and future results of this long-running "Disarmament Conference" can all be recognized and predicted.

Originally, in the current stage of the situation, trying to achieve any "disarmament" or "arms reduction" is truly wishful thinking and self-deception. Under such a "conference," the imperialist powers are all based on the principle of expanding their own armaments while cutting those of other countries. Furthermore, the fact that some "alliances" and "conventions" in the recent past and still continuing were disregarded and almost completely destroyed by Japanese imperialism serves as the best comparison and clear evidence. Therefore, "Another world war is coming!" This is what many people are worried about. But is the Second World War inevitable? Where do its possibilities and causes lie? To understand these things, one can only start from the objective conditions of the historical process.

As we already know, because many backward countries have been swept into the vortex of world capitalism, this has created the possibility of capital exports by capitalist countries. At the same time, because capitalist countries have long reached "excessive maturity," and their capital (which of course first lies in the underdevelopment of their agriculture and the poverty of the masses) has long been insufficient for its "profitable" investment markets, this has created the necessity of capital exports, which is why the capitalist powers are "making persistent efforts," "greedily unquenchable," "competing with each other" to seize their "profitable" investment markets, sales markets, and sources of raw materials. This is also the development and seizure of colonies. Of course, the commercial war of capitalist countries to seize high profit rates must be prepared for military war. But since one must prepare for military war, one must work harder to enrich the sources of wealth through commercial war. Therefore, the military armaments of capitalist countries are becoming increasingly competitive. And their commercial wars are becoming more and more fierce, and in the end, they can only be temporarily resolved with a shocking military war. However, the internal and mutual contradictions of capitalist countries can only become more and more acute under this situation and can never be resolved. The fact that the situation between capitalist countries such as Germany, France, Britain, and Russia during the First World War in 1914 and their current situation remains irreconcilable is excellent evidence. (To be continued)

A Glimpse of the Kalachakra Tantra Assembly 251

— He Juefu

I boarded the bus to Lingyin Temple on a drizzly morning. Although it was morning, the goose-feather-like fine rain was falling incessantly; however, devout men and women pilgrims were still walking on the muddy path in a continuous stream like clouds.

Getting off the bus and stepping into the main gate of Lingyin Temple, I looked up at the yellow paper slogans plastered all over the walls on both sides, the armed comrades standing tall beside the road and at every doorway with long guns and bayonets, and the archways across the road with large white characters "Welcome XX..." hanging on them. You would always suspect that you had gone the wrong way and mistakenly entered a celebration or welcome rally for some dignitary. However, as soon as you walked into the first main hall, the scene changed completely. Here, although several soldiers with long guns and bayonets also stood on both sides of the front door, all that could be seen inside were the god-like clay statues, curling incense smoke, flickering candlelight, and devout men and women pilgrims kneeling and worshiping. It seemed that the prosperity of the incense was unprecedented since the opening of the temple!

Passing through the main hall, what towered in front was a magnificent grand hall. There, it was where our masters and lamas set up altars and chanted scriptures. On both sides of the corridor leading to the main hall, several guards were guarding, and tourists were not allowed to go up at will. When I stepped straight in, I was stopped by a guard who asked:

"Do you have an admission ticket?"

"No!" I replied respectfully.

"You can't go in without an admission ticket; however, if you are anxious to take a look, you can go to the general affairs office to ask for one," he said, pointing to a small room in the corridor.

I followed the direction he pointed and went to the general affairs office, where I saw the large characters "Admission ticket not for sale" posted on the wall, and I thought to myself. Maybe you can get it by saying a few oath-like words, right? However, when I told the clerk about my intention, he took out several notebooks from the drawer and placed them in front of me; and said with a smile very gently.

"Yes, not for sale; however, there is a small restriction. That is, whoever wants to save the souls of the dead or seek blessings for themselves can donate one or ten yuan at will to cover the expenses of this association, and they can get a free ticket. If anyone can come and take it at will, then there is no need to spend a lot of money to print these things. Sir, what do you think? Just write your name here, are you seeking blessings for yourself?"

After listening to his words, I didn't say anything, because I couldn't afford to spend so much money; but. Looking at the crowded tourists and pilgrims above, I was indeed a little moved. I seemed to have lost my judgment, just wandering and pondering in the corridor!

It was thanks to God's blessing that a young man working here saw my hesitant appearance, walked up to my side, and said softly in my ear:

"Give me two dimes, and I'll lend you one; however, this is my personal one, you have to return it to me after you've finished watching it above!"

"Thank you!" For two dimes, I could see many new things, and of course I was very happy to do so. I immediately took out two dimes and gave it to him, and quickly walked up the steps to the main hall.

The entrance of the hall was tightly packed with a large crowd of onlookers, and it took me a lot of effort to squeeze in. Inside, piled in the center was the golden body of our Buddha Tathagata, below the golden body was the seat of our master, and on both sides of the master were seated more than a dozen lamas. In front of them were placed many Tibetan Buddhist scriptures and instruments such as horns and reeds. Under the command of the master, everyone took the same rhythm and the same tune, chanting "La Ya Sha..." After chanting, they played a piece of Tibetan (?) music. It looked very devout. I squeezed tightly in the crowd and watched intently for more than an hour, always chanting scriptures and playing music in succession; I didn't see any new tricks, and I really felt bored. I secretly paid a salute to the master, squeezed out of the crowd, and embarked on the way home.

On the way back, I was always thinking silently like this. After our suffering sentient beings have been so painstakingly prayed for by the master, who would dare not believe that they can be saved?

— Meng

Fengchun and Guiying discussed it for a while: the only way is to abandon this home village exploited by corrupt officials and gentry and seek a happy land elsewhere. (The End)

Talking About Contradiction 253

— Zhenqiu

A spear and a shield, viewed separately, do not harmonize. If everything in the world could proceed smoothly, without any obstacles in the middle to cause trouble, contradictions would not arise. For example, if we were living in a prosperous feudal era, we would follow the systems and habits of the old society without any scruples, and we would not find it strange for anyone to burn incense and worship Buddha, or for scholars to raise concubines. But after the feudal society, a capitalist society came along, which is what is called an obstacle in the middle causing trouble. We would then find it contradictory to see a ten-story building on Nanjing Road standing next to an antique "Rainbow Temple" from the Middle Ages under the massive influence of capital; it would also be a contradictory phenomenon to see a few women with bound feet and long hair in the midst of a trend where women's clothing competes to expose the chest and legs. If someone at this time were to read Zhao Ziyue's and Mencius's sayings and try to take the imperial examination and become a top scholar, they would be scolded as being old-fashioned, outdated, and unfit to be human! Therefore, the so-called contradiction comes entirely from disharmony, and disharmony is entirely the result of changes in the times.

However, in the Chinese saying that "heroes create the times," the basis of contradiction in "temporal error" is not established. Heroes can create the times, and changes in the times can lead to contradictions, so isn't contradiction indirectly created by human power? Therefore, contradiction becomes something in people's heads, and eventually, people gradually forget its true source.

Originally, Confucius's Doctrine of the Mean in China called on people to achieve a "middle ground," and it was not necessary to reveal contradictions very obviously. It was best to handle everything ambiguously and cleverly, which was especially in line with art. A great man would not easily show his unhappiness on the outside, and would still maintain a calm attitude on the surface; Ah Q could console himself by comparing himself to the "father" of the person who beat him. Therefore, contradictions in China have long been incorporated into the cultivation of the Doctrine of the Mean by the Chinese people.

For example, if Fascism enters China, and someone praises it as a political ideology that is "the trend of the world," can you criticize them for praising it unreasonably? Therefore, this statement also has great artistic attainments.

There is simply no contradiction to speak of in China. Contradiction is dissolved by the broad and profound cultivation of the Chinese nation. Because the Chinese people's thought of the Mean is consistent, contradiction in China恰恰 becomes "unity." This is precisely what is created by "heroes creating the times."

Women's Common Diseases 255

— Xiao Cen

Everyone says that women have several common diseases. Such as vanity, stinginess, jealousy, dependence, passivity

Page 19

and so on. I also think it's good, it seems difficult to deny. If you don't believe it, we can see: how many women in society fall into deep pain for the sake of vanity; for the sake of stinginess and jealousy, various meaningless conflicts and misunderstandings occur and lead to tragedy; not even applying a little powder to please men, eventually becoming other people's toys; good dependence and passive behavior lead to the formation of a weak woman with no will. Especially a very revolutionary woman with profound knowledge, if she falls in love with a counter-revolutionary man, as a result, she also goes to do counter-revolutionary work, perhaps abandoning the important responsibility of revolution and willing to retreat to the corrupt old society to live a life of dependence, jealousy, quarrel, pleasing, and hypocrisy. I think this further exposes the weakness of women's inability to move upward. We are not saying that every woman must suffer from this weakness and disease, at least 90 percent of them are like this.

In fact, this common disease is not only understood by men, women themselves also know it very well, but they are not willing to treat it! They always seem to be willing to have no days of standing out, not reviewing their own shortcomings, and even losing their temper when criticized. Such a lack of self-respect, it seems no wonder that for thousands of years, they have been oppressed! History clearly tells us that women have always been bullied in society. It is true that we attribute this to the poor social system of the past. Therefore, after the Qing Dynasty was overthrown, until the time of the May Fourth Movement, the clamor for women's liberation was shouted for a long time; this was obviously a great opportunity for women to save themselves. But this clamor is still only a clamor after all, it cannot become very practical, so that women can obtain true liberation and obtain a truly equal social status from that time on. Regarding this, we cannot but say that on the one hand, it is the fault of this society, they implement deceptive education, they are not willing to guide them to realize their due rights in society: and on the other hand, we cannot but say that women themselves do not know how to cherish themselves, self-respect to remove their own diseases, climbing the road forward and working hard to move upward, they let others call out injustices for her, but they do not care, let this clamor slowly sink in the air. Keeping women's status in the same attitude as in the past, or it can be said that it has lost its value more than before! In the past, women were still able to manage the family finances, which was considered to have fulfilled their share of human responsibility, and now the so-called new women, who have read many years of Chinese and foreign texts, do not know what they can contribute to society? Although society cannot give them opportunities, at least they must first respect and examine themselves, remove the unconscious demon diseases, enrich their own academic foundation, and prepare for struggle.

Movie Special Issue, Republic of China 23rd Year, May 9th, Wednesday

On Soviet Renowned Director Eisenstein's Film Script Theory 258

— Gaoyuan

In the preface to the film script "The Entire Line" (全綫), co-authored by Eisenstein and Alexandrov, Eisenstein expressed the following opinions regarding the form a film script should take, clarifying the scope of work for film scriptwriters and directors. Not long ago, our film industry also sparked a debate on whether the work of scriptwriters and directors should be handled by one person. Now, I will translate the main points below for reference.

A film script distinguished by numbers is as repetitive as the numbers arranged at the feet of corpses and cannot produce a film.

In essence, a film script is not the formation of material, but a stage in the process of material formation. A film script exists as a stage between a chosen theme digested by emotion (Temperament) and its visual embodiment.

A film script is not a stage script.

A drama, even without an effective stage performance, still has independent value. A drama still has the value of being a permanent reading material. Conversely, a film script seeks its own concretization in countless visual forms, a shorthand for emotional expression.

A film script is merely a bottle of wine that exists to suddenly pull the cork, allowing champagne-like emotions to flow into a parched throat.

A film script is a signal from one emotion to another.

The film scriptwriter gives the film script a perceptual rhythm with his unique technique.

The director participates in this, transplanting this perceptual rhythm into the director's own unique language, that is, the language of film.

Director 丨丨

Discovers the film's equivalent to that which should change the literary report.

The root of the problem lies here, not in the sequential order of shots or the continuous narrative of events in the script.

Our requirements for film scripts are simply this; this view strikes a fatal blow to the form of "shooting scripts" that have always been marked with numbers one by one.

The worst case for a film script is when it is written by an ordinary craftsman; such a film script is merely a repetitive and visual description of what is to be shown to the audience.

However, the secret lies in forming a chain of experiences to be presented to the audience through the film script.

When exploring the organized creation of such a film script, we then arrive at the form of the film novel.

According to this form, what we aim for is to clearly express in words on paper what will be provided on the screen丨丨, for example, by means of a herd of livestock, sunsets, waterfalls, or endless wilderness. Our so-called film novel is, in essence, the same as replicating the story that will greatly excite and move the audience who will see that film in the future. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Wharf Angel" 丨Grand Theater丨 259

— Ling He

Although this is also based on the theme of a love triangle, this "Wharf Angel" should be outstanding among the many American films with the same theme.

We are not merely giving it a higher evaluation because everything expressed in the work is very close to the sentimental feelings of the Chinese people. On the contrary, if we carefully grasp the entire work, then we admit that the two directors of this drama have had a full understanding of the conflict and contradiction between love and friendship that the playwright wanted to express and have faithfully expressed them.

The conflict between friendship and love is perhaps a phenomenon that we can often see. However, what we should pay attention to now is the playwright's precise description of the story's development process, dramatically emphasizing each scene's psychological changes, which should be the first characteristic of this work. And all of these depend on the genuine skills of each actor, which goes without saying.

Secondly, because the playwright first had a meticulous structure for the script, the dramatic connections between each scene and each scene clearly show the achievements of film art. Naturally, this is mainly due to the director's contributions. He gives us a clear and understanding feeling; no waste, no rambling, which is the characteristic of his expression methods.

Yes, from the director's montage, from the composition of the shots, from the description of the surrounding atmosphere, from the grasp of the drama's Tempo, and from the expression of the personalities of the characters in the drama, all aspects can prove that the director has rich creative experience and literary cultivation.

However, there are still some shortcomings in the story's development. For example, in writing about Toy and Como's night in the upstairs room, we don't feel that it is a deep and strong love, and this love occurs in a prostitute, so how Toy is loyal to love afterward inevitably makes people feel unnatural. This is to say that the previous setting is quite insufficient. Secondly, after Como is arrested, a very tragic climax could have been triggered from the prostitute Toy, such as shouting and crying as she watches him being taken into prison, which could give people a deeper impression, at least more powerful than the final scene of talking through the iron gate. However, this is the influence of American films, although this ending is not how happy, it also gives people a feeling of endless regret, but after all, it is not the ending method that this film should have.

However, this is a concrete expression of the playwright's ideology. It is very clear that in addition to the conflict between friendship and love, it also writes about the cruelty of the law. But that is by no means the theme, regardless of whether he also expresses dissatisfaction with the law. Therefore, if this point is used as the theme at the end, it will definitely give the audience the most profound and tragic impression from the law and the police. On the contrary, precisely because the playwright dares not attack the unreasonableness of the current social law, and also feels that prisons and the police are terrible things after all, he has to justify himself and explain it to mean that the person who sells his friend for a woman uses the bounty he got from the police station to hire a lawyer for the prisoner. That is to say, the law is always just, not to mention that it maintains the existence of the law. In addition, regarding the theme constituted by the conflict between friendship and love, the playwright emphasizes the internal conflict between the two friends, so he says that Duke's betrayal was entirely to vent his anger, not to covet the reward of one thousand yuan, which may not give us a more real feeling. Therefore, it also makes us think that this story conforms to the cliché that "no coincidence, no story." However, to say one more thing, this drama is quite close to the living feelings of the Chinese people.

A Glimpse through a Circular Mirror by Louis Stone

Audience Opinion

Watching "Pear Blossoms in a Rainstorm" 261

— Gu Yue

"Pear Blossoms in a Rainstorm" is clearly a tragedy, a tragedy that satirizes life, even more profound and moving than the depiction in "Life."

Xiao Ying likes to eat bread, Xiao Qin likes to eat rice; Xiao Ying envies the brightly lit city, but Xiao Qin is blind, so Xiao Ying is ultimately seduced, which is a very good omen.

When Xiao Ying returns home to see her sister after being seduced, she is wearing silk clothes, but what her sister touches is cloth, which is clearly Xiao Ying deceiving her, but how can Xiao Ying think at this time that people are deceiving her in the same way that she is deceiving her sister? Life is originally a deception, which is a very good contrast and satire.

Speaking of the performance aspects, everyone inevitably has inappropriate expressions.

Xiao Ying's expression when she is seduced to Shi's house is extremely difficult. But she thinks about it scene by scene and can handle it, which is a success.

Xiao Qin is blind, and a blind person's eyes cannot move. Of course, everyone admits that Xiao Qin is a very difficult role to play. There are several inner expressions that are also quite successful.

Gao Zhanfei is beyond criticism because he is basically a supporting role, I think. He Feiguang is playing a villain, but he is not as good as Yuan Congmei's villain.

What we cannot forget the most is an unknown little sister inside, she has very lively expressions, I think she is promising, I hope the United Photoplay Service can cultivate her well.

"Pear Blossoms in a Rainstorm" depicts a pair of sisters, a pair of sisters with different ideas and different experiences, which has a satirical meaning compared to the Star Film Company's "Sisters Flowers." I believe that the plot of "Rainstorm Blossoms" is more profound and intense than "Sisters Flowers." At least! It can be called the "Sisters Flowers."

Film Novel

The House of Rothschild (10) (6) 263

— Wen Yin

Nathan listened to his brothers, pondered for a long time, and then declared: "Amschel, everything you say is correct..."

"...Your ideas are all right... Every word you say is reasonable... But丨 we must defeat Napoleon!" James asked in confusion: "What's the reason?" Nathan then stood up and calmly explained the reason. He said: "What's the reason? Because we are members of the Rothschild family... At present, we are not just five wealthy Jews seeking great opportunities. We need to know that the whole world knows that whether you are Jewish or not, Europe will not have peace until Napoleon is gone. This is a fact you cannot deny!" Gudula was overjoyed and leaned her body against Nathan. Then Nathan spoke again: "We must take some risks. We can only endure for a while 丨 and not be impulsed by some selfish desires and feelings 丨 to do our best for the benefit of the world. We can unite with Napoleon and let him continue to fight for ten or eight years. Our money can be used to buy weapons and blood, until the whole of Europe becomes a massacre ground 丨 but what benefits will the Jews get? Isn't it just a lifelong pawnshop business? We must not do that 丨 we must strive for peace, as before, but we must not help the war. If we must perish, we must perish with honor. We cannot leave any shame behind us 丨 no matter what position!"

After listening to Nathan's words, Gudula happily placed her withered hand on Nathan's hand and said, "My son, these are the words your father would have said." Then Amschel, Solomon, Carl, James, and the other four brothers seemed to suddenly realize something, looking at each other, their hearts filled with brotherly love and racial glory. Amschel was the first to say, "I agree with Nathan's words." The four of them rushed to shake hands with Nathan, and Carl patted him on the shoulder. Nathan was so emotionally overwhelmed that he couldn't speak, and he just swallowed the word "thank you." His eyes were wet with tears.

Led by Colonel Fitzroy, Prince Metternich, Duke Retland, and Duke Talleyrand actually lowered their status and visited the Jewish street in Frankfurt to visit Rothschild. Nathan formally received them, and everyone held a meeting. Metternich frankly expressed his shame to Nathan, saying, "Nathan, we know that we have treated you in many wrong ways. Now I can frankly say that we need your help." Retland stubbornly interjected, "That's not how it is said. The Allied countries are waiting to use money. We are not here to ask you to give alms. You are a lender, and we will give you interest." Nathan said, "Am I sure I want to lend money to you?" Solomon said from the side, "Austria is already bankrupt." James also said, "France is already in Napoleon's hands." Carl added, "Italy is no exception." Solomon said again, "What if Napoleon wins?" Metternich explained, "Of course, whatever you do, you always have to take some risks." (To be continued)
